 product.description.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          product.tags.some(tag => tag.toLowerCase().includes(query)) ||\n          product.supplier.name.toLowerCase().includes(query);\n        if (!matchesSearch) return false;\n      }\n\n      // Category filter\n      if (filters.category && product.category !== filters.category) return false;\n\n      // Subcategory filter\n      if (filters.subcategory && product.subcategory !== filters.subcategory) return false;\n\n      // Price range filter\n      const price = product.price.discounted;\n      if (price < filters.priceRange[0] || price > filters.priceRange[1]) return false;\n\n      // Rating filter\n      if (product.rating.average < filters.minRating) return false;\n\n      // Supplier location filter\n      if (filters.supplierLocation.length > 0 && \n          !filters.supplierLocation.includes(product.supplier.location.country)) return false;\n\n      // Free shipping filter\n      if (filters.freeShipping && !product.shipping.freeShipping) return false;\n\n      // Verified supplier filter\n      if (filters.verifiedSupplier && !product.supplier.isVerified) return false;\n\n      // In stock filter\n      if (filters.inStock && product.stock <= 0) return false;\n\n      // MOQ filter\n      if (product.moq > filters.moqMax) return false;\n\n      // Tags filter\n      if (filters.tags.length > 0 && !filters.tags.some(tag => product.tags.includes(tag))) return false;\n\n      return true;\n    });\n\n    // Apply sorting\n    filtered = filtered.sort((a, b) => {\n      switch (sortBy) {\n        case \'price-low\':\n          return a.price.discounted - b.price.discounted;\n        case \'price-high\':\n          return b.price.discounted - a.price.discounted;\n        case \'rating\':\n          return b.rating.average - a.rating.average;\n        case \'orders\':\n          return b.orders - a.orders;\n        default:\n          return 0;\n      }\n    });\n\n => {\n      const existingItem = prev.find(item => item.id === product.id);\n      if (existingItem) {\n        return prev.map(item =>\n          item.id === product.id\n            ? { ...item,      ? prev.filter(id => id !== productId)\n        : [...prev, productId]\n    );\n  }, []);\n\n  // Calculate cart totals\n  const cartTotal = cart.reduce((total, item) => total + (item.price.discounted * item.quantity), 0);\n  const cartItemsCount = cart.reduce((total, item) => total + item.quantity, 0);\n\n  // Format price\n  const formatPrice = (price: number, currency: text-yellow-400" />);\n    }\n    for (let i = stars.length; i < 5; i++) {\n      stars.push(<Star key={i} className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-300" />);\n    }\n    return stars;\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg border border-gray-200">\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">\n        <div className="flex items-center lastPasswordChange: \'2023-11-01\',\n      loginAttempts: 1,\n      deviceTrust: []\n    },\n    status: \'active\',\n    roles: [\'user\'],\n    permissions: [\'buy\'],\n    notes: \'New user, exploring the platform\',\n    tags: [\'new\', \'free\'],\n    createdAt: \'2023-11-01T11:00:00Z\',\n    updatedAt: \'2024-01-18T16:45:00Z\'\n  }\n];\n\nconst SUBSCRIPTION_TIERS = [\n  { tier: \'free\', name: \'Free\', color: \'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700\', icon: Users },\n  { tier: \'basic\', name: \'Basic\', color: \'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700\', icon: Shield },\n  { tier: \'premium\', name: \'Premium\', color: \'bg-purple-100 text-purple-700\', icon: Crown },\n  { tier: \'enterprise\', name: \'Enterprise\', color: \'bg-orange-100 text-orange-700\', icon: Gem }\n];\n\nconst USER_ROLES = [\n  { role: \'user\', name: \'User\', description: \'Regular platform user\' },\n  { role: \'seller\', name: \'Seller\', description: \'Can list and sell products\' },\n  { role: \'moderator\', name: \'Moderator\', description: \'Can moderate content\' },\n  { role: \'admin\', name: \'Administrator\', description: \'Full system access\' }\n];\n\nexport const UserManagementSystem: React.FC = () => {\n  const [users, setUsers] = useState<UserProfile[]>(MOCK_USERS);\n  const [filteredUsers, setFilteredUsers] = useState<UserProfile[]>(MOCK_USERS);\n  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState<UserProfile | null>(null);\n  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState(\'\');\n  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<UserFilter>({\n    status: \'\',\n    subscriptionTier: \'\',\n    verification: \'\',\n    country: \'\',\n    joinDateRange: [\'\', \'\'],\n    lastLoginRange: [\'\', \'\'],\n    hasOrders: false,\n    hasProducts: false,\n    minSpent: 0,\n    maxSpent: 100000,\n    tags: []\n  });\n  const [showFilters, setShowFilters] = useState(false);\n  const [showCreateUser, setShowCreateUser] = useState(false);\n  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);\n  const [showUserDetails, setShowUserDetails] = useState(false);\n  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);\n\n  // Apply filters and search\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let filtered = users.filter(user => {\n      // Search query\n      if (searchQuery) {\n        const query = searchQuery.toLowerCase();\n        const matchesSearch = \n          user.username.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          user.email.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          `${user.firstName} ${user.lastName}`.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          user.location.city.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          user.location.country.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||\n          user.tags.some(tag => tag.toLowerCase().includes(query));\n        if (!matchesSearch) return false;\n      }\n\n      // Status filter\n      if (filters.status && user.status !== filters.status) return false;\n\n      // Subscription tier filter\n      if (filters.subscriptionTier && user.subscription.tier !== filters.subscriptionTier) return false;\n\n      // Verification filter\n      if (filters.verification) {\n        if (filters.verification === \'email\' && !user.verification.email) return false;\n        if (filters.verification === \'phone\' && !user.verification.phone) return false;\n        if (filters.verification === \'identity\' && !user.verification.identity) return false;\n        if (filters.verification === \'business\' && !user.verification.business) return false;\n      }\n\n      // Country filter\n      if (filters.country && user.location.country !== filters.country) return false;\n\n      // Date filters would need more complex implementation\n      // For brevity, skipping detailed date filtering logic\n\n      // Has orders filter\n      if (filters.hasOrders && user.statistics.totalOrders === 0) return false;\n\n      // Has products filter\n      if (filters.hasProducts && user.statistics.productsListed === 0) return false;\n\n      // Spending range filter\n      if (user.statistics.totalSpent < filters.minSpent || user.statistics.totalSpent > filters.maxSpent) return false;\n\n      // Tags filter\n      if (filters.tags.length > 0 && !filters.tags.some(tag => user.tags.includes(tag))) return false;\n\n      return true;\n    });\n\n    setFilteredUsers(filtered);\n  }, [users, searchQuery, filters]);\n\n  // Get subscription tier info\n  const getSubscriptionTier = (tier: string) => {\n    return SUBSCRIPTION_TIERS.find(t => t.tier === tier) || SUBSCRIPTION_TIERS[0];\n  };\n\n  // Get status color\n  const getStatusColor = (status: string): string => {\n    switch (status) {\n      case \'active\': return \'bg-green-100 text-green-800\';\n      case \'inactive\': return \'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800\';\n      case \'suspended\': return \'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800\';\n      case \'banned\': return \'bg-red-100 text-red-800\';\n      default: return \'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800\';\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Get verification status\n  const getVerificationStatus = (verification: UserProfile[\'verification\']): { status: string; color: string } => {\n    const verifiedCount = Object.values(verification).filter(v => v).length;\n    const totalVerifications = Object.keys(verification).length;\n    \n    if (verifiedCount === totalVerifications) {\n      return { status: \'Fully Verified\', color: \'bg-green-100 text-green-800\' };\n    } else if (verifiedCount >= 3) {\n      return { status: \'Partially Verified\', color: \'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800\' };\n    } else if (verifiedCount >= 1) {\n      return { status: \'Basic Verification\', color: \'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800\' };\n    } else {\n      return { status: \'Not Verified\', color: \'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800\' };\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Format currency\n  const formatCurrency = (amount: number, currency: string = \'USD\'): string => {\n    return new Intl.NumberFormat(\'en-US\', {\n      style: \'currency\',\n      currency: currency\n    }).format(amount);\n  };\n\n  // Toggle user status\n  const toggleUserStatus = useCallback(async (userId: string, newStatus: UserProfile[\'status\']) => {\n    setUsers(prev => prev.map(user =>\n      user.id === userId ? { ...user, status: newStatus } : user\n    ));\n  }, []);\n\n  // Reset user password\n  const resetUserPassword = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {\n    // Mock password reset\n    alert(\'Password reset link sent to user email\');\n  }, []);\n\n  // Send verification email\n  const sendVerificationEmail = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {\n    // Mock verification email\n    alert(\'Verification email sent to user\');\n  }, []);\n\n  // Delete user\n  const deleteUser = useCallback(async (userId: string) => {\n    if (confirm(\'Are you sure you want to delete this user? This action cannot be undone.\')) {\n      setUsers(prev => prev.filter(user => user.id !== userId));\n      if (selectedUser?.id === userId) {\n        setSelectedUser(null);\n        setShowUserDetails(false);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [selectedUser]);\n\n  return (\n    <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg border border-gray-200">\n      {/* Header */}\n      <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">\n        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">\n          <div>\n            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900 flex items-center">\n              <Users className="w-5 h-5 mr-2 text-blue-500" />\n              User Management System\n            </h2>\n            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">\n              Comprehensive user profiles, verification, and management\n            </p>\n          </div>\n          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n            <button className="px-4 py-2 bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-200">\n              <Download className="w-4 h-4 inline mr-2" />\n              Export\n            </button>\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setShowCreateUser(true)}\n              className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700"\n            >\n              <UserPlus className="w-4 h-4 inline mr-2" />\n              Create User\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Search and Filters */}\n      <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200 bg-gray-50">\n        <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-4">\n          {/* Search Bar */}\n          <div className="flex-1">\n            <div className="relative">\n              <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400 w-5 h-5" />\n              <input\n                type="text"\n                placeholder="Search users by name, email, username, or location..."\n                value={searchQuery}\n                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}\n                className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Quick Filters */}\n          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n            <select\n              value={filters.status}\n              onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, status: e.target.value }))}\n              className="px-4 py-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n            >\n              <option value="">All Status</option>\n              <option value="active">Active</option>\n              <option value="inactive">Inactive</option>\n              <option value="suspended">Suspended</option>\n              <option value="banned">Banned</option>\n            </select>\n\n            <select\n              value={filters.subscriptionTier}\n              onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, subscriptionTier: e.target.value }))}\n              className="px-4 py-3 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n            >\n              <option value="">All Tiers</option>\n              {SUBSCRIPTION_TIERS.map(tier => (\n                <option key={tier.tier} value={tier.tier}>{tier.name}</option>\n              ))}\n            </select>\n\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setShowFilters(!showFilters)}\n              className={`px-4 py-3 rounded-lg ${showFilters ? \'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700\' : \'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700\'}`}\n            >\n              <Filter className="w-4 h-4 inline mr-2" />\n              Filters\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Advanced Filters */}\n        {showFilters && (\n          <div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-white rounded-lg border border-gray-200">\n            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">\n              {/* Country Filter */}\n              <div>\n                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">Country</label>\n                <select\n                  value={filters.country}\n                  onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, country: e.target.value }))}\n                  className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n                >\n                  <option value="">All Countries</option>\n                  <option value="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</option>\n                  <option value="UAE">UAE</option>\n                  <option value="Egypt">Egypt</option>\n                  <option value="USA">USA</option>\n                  <option value="UK">UK</option>\n                </select>\n              </div>\n\n              {/* Verification Filter */}\n              <div>\n                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">Verification Status</label>\n                <select\n                  value={filters.verification}\n                  onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, verification: e.target.value }))}\n                  className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n                >\n                  <option value="">All Levels</option>\n                  <option value="email">Email Verified</option>\n                  <option value="phone">Phone Verified</option>\n                  <option value="identity">Identity Verified</option>\n                  <option value="business">Business Verified</option>\n                </select>\n              </div>\n\n              {/* Activity Filters */}\n              <div>\n                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">Activity</label>\n                <div className="space-y-2">\n                  <label className="flex items-center">\n                    <input\n                      type="checkbox"\n                      checked={filters.hasOrders}\n                      onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, hasOrders: e.target.checked }))}\n                      className="mr-2"\n                    />\n                    <span className="text-sm">Has Orders</span>\n                  </label>\n                  <label className="flex items-center">\n                    <input\n                      type="checkbox"\n                      checked={filters.hasProducts}\n                      onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, hasProducts: e.target.checked }))}\n                      className="mr-2"\n                    />\n                    <span className="text-sm">Has Products</span>\n                  </label>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              {/* Spending Range */}\n              <div>\n                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">\n                  Total Spending: {formatCurrency(filters.minSpent)} - {formatCurrency(filters.maxSpent)}\n                </label>\n                <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n                  <input\n                    type="number"\n                    value={filters.minSpent}\n                    onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, minSpent: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0 }))}\n                    className="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n                    placeholder="Min"\n                  />\n                  <span className="text-gray-500">-</span>\n                  <input\n                    type="number"\n                    value={filters.maxSpent}\n                    onChange={(e) => setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, maxSpent: parseInt(e.target.value) || 100000 }))}\n                    className="flex-1 px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"\n                    placeholder="Max"\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className="mt-4 flex justify-end">\n              <button\n                onClick={() => setFilters({\n                  status: \'\',\n                  subscriptionTier: \'\',\n                  verification: \'\',\n                  country: \'\',\n                  joinDateRange: [\'\', \'\'],\n                  lastLoginRange: [\'\', \'\'],\n                  hasOrders: false,\n                  hasProducts: false,\n                  minSpent: 0,\n                  maxSpent: 100000,\n                  tags: []\n                })}\n                className="px-4 py-2 text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-800"\n              >\n                Clear All Filters\n              </button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Results Summary */}\n      <div className="px-6 py-3 border-b border-gray-200">\n        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">\n          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">\n            Showing {filteredUsers.length} of {users.length} users\n          </p>\n          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n            <button className="text-sm text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-700">\n              <RefreshCw className="w-3 h-3 inline mr-1" />\n              Refresh\n            </button>\n            <button className="text-sm text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-700">\n              <Upload className="w-3 h-3 inline mr-1" />\n              Import Users\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Users List */}\n      <div className="overflow-x-auto">\n        <table className="w-full">\n          <thead className="bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-200">\n            <tr>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                User\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Status\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Subscription\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Verification\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Statistics\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Last Login\n              </th>\n              <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">\n                Actions\n              </th>\n            </tr>\n          </thead>\n          <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">\n            {filteredUsers.map(user => {\n              const tierInfo = getSubscriptionTier(user.subscription.tier);\n              const verificationInfo = getVerificationStatus(user.verification);\n              const TierIcon = tierInfo.icon;\n\n              return (\n                <tr key={user.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">\n                    <div className="flex items-center">\n                      <div className="flex-shrink-0 h-10 w-10">\n                        <img\n                          className="h-10 w-10 rounded-full object-cover"\n                          src={user.avatar || \'https://via.placeholder.com/40\'}\n                          alt={user.username}\n                        />\n                      </div>\n                      <div className="ml-4">\n                        <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">\n                          {user.firstName} {user.lastName}\n                        </div>\n                        <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">@{user.username}</div>\n                        <div className="text-xs text-gray-400 flex items-center mt-1">\n                          <Mail className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />\n                          {user.email}\n                        </div>\n                        <div className="text-xs text-gray-400 flex items-center">\n                          <MapPin className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />\n                          {user.location.city}, {user.location.country}\n                        </div>\n                      </div>\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">\n                    <span className={`px-2 py-1 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getStatusColor(user.status)}`}>\n                      {user.status}\n                    </span>\n                    {user.roles.includes(\'seller\') && (\n                      <span className="ml-2 px-2 py-1 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full bg-blue-100 text-blue-800">\n                        Seller\n                      </span>\n                    )}\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">\n                    <div className="flex items-center">\n                      <div className={`flex items-center px-2 py-1 rounded-lg text-xs font-medium ${tierInfo.color}`}>\n                        <TierIcon className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />\n                        {tierInfo.name}\n                      </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <div className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">\n                      {user.subscription.status === \'active\' ? (\n                        <span className="text-green-600">Active</span>\n                      ) : (\n                        <span className="text-red-600">{user.subscription.status}</span>\n                      )}\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">\n                    <div className={`px-2 py-1 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${verificationInfo.color}`}>\n                      {verificationInfo.status}\n                    </div>\n                    <div className="flex space-x-1 mt-1">\n                      {user.verification.email && <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-green-500" title="Email verified" />}\n                      {user.verification.phone && <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-green-500" title="Phone verified" />}\n                      {user.verification.identity && <Shield className="w-3 h-3 text-blue-500" title="Identity verified" />}\n                      {user.verification.business && <Award className="w-3 h-3 text-purple-500" title="Business verified" />}\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">\n                    <div className="space-y-1">\n                      <div>{user.statistics.totalOrders} orders</div>\n                      <div>{formatCurrency(user.statistics.totalSpent, user.preferences.currency)}</div>\n                      <div className="flex items-center">\n                        <Star className="w-3 h-3 text-yellow-500 mr-1" />\n                        {user.statistics.reputation.toFixed(1)} ({user.statistics.reviewsReceived} reviews)\n                      </div>\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-500">\n                    <div className="flex items-center">\n                      <Clock className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />\n                      {new Date(user.statistics.lastLogin).toLocaleDateString()}\n                    </div>\n                    <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">\n                      {new Date(user.statistics.lastLogin).toLocaleTimeString()}\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n\n                  <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">\n                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => {\n                          setSelectedUser(user);\n                          setShowUserDetails(true);\n                          setEditMode(false);\n                        }}\n                        className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900"\n                        title="View Details"\n                      >\n                        <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />\n                      </button>\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => {\n                          setSelectedUser(user);\n                          setShowUserDetails(true);\n                          setEditMode(true);\n                        }}\n                        className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900"\n                        title="Edit User"\n                      >\n                        <Edit className="w-4 h-4" />\n                      </button>\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => resetUserPassword(user.id)}\n                        className="text-yellow-600 hover:text-yellow-900"\n                        title="Reset Password"\n                      >\n                        <Lock className="w-4 h-4" />\n                      </button>\n                      {user.status === \'active\' ? (\n                        <button\n                          onClick={() => toggleUserStatus(user.id, \'suspended\')}\n                          className="text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-900"\n                          title="Suspend User"\n                        >\n                          <AlertTriangle className="w-4 h-4" />\n                        </button>\n                      ) : (\n                        <button\n                          onClick={() => toggleUserStatus(user.id, \'active\')}\n                          className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900"\n                          title="Activate User"\n                        >\n                          <CheckCircle className="w-4 h-4" />\n                        </button>\n                      )}\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => deleteUser(user.id)}\n                        className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900"\n                        title="Delete User"\n                      >\n                        <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />\n                      </button>\n                    </div>\n                  </td>\n                </tr>\n              );\n            })}\n          </tbody>\n        </table>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* User Details Modal */}\n      {showUserDetails && selectedUser && (\n        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50 p-4">\n          <div className="bg-white rounded-xl max-w-4xl w-full max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto">\n            <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">\n              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">\n                <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900">\n                  User Details - {selectedUser.firstName} {selectedUser.lastName}\n                </h3>\n                <button\n                  onClick={() => setShowUserDetails(false)}\n                  className="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"\n                >\n                  <X className="w-5 h-5" />\n                </button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className="p-6">\n              {/* User Profile Header */}\n              <div className="flex items-start space-x-6 mb-6">\n                <div className="flex-shrink-0">\n                  <img\n                    className="h-20 w-20 rounded-full object-cover"\n                    src={selectedUser.avatar || \'https://via.placeholder.com/80\'}\n                    alt={selectedUser.username}\n                  />\n                </div>\n                <div className="flex-1">\n                  <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">\n                    <h4 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">\n                      {selectedUser.firstName} {selectedUser.lastName}\n                    </h4>\n                    <span className={`px-2 py-1 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getStatusColor(selectedUser.status)}`}>\n                      {selectedUser.status}\n                    </span>\n                  </div>\n                  <p className="text-gray-600">@{selectedUser.username}</p>\n                  <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">\n                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-600">\n                      <Mail className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />\n                      {selectedUser.email}\n                    </div>\n                    {selectedUser.phone && (\n                      <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-600">\n                        <Phone className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />\n                        {selectedUser.phone}\n                      </div>\n                    )}\n                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-600">\n                      <MapPin className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />\n                      {selectedUser.location.city}, {selectedUser.location.country}\n                    </div>\n                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-600">\n DEFAULT 0.00,\n    total_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT \'USD\',\n    \n    -- Shipping information\n    shipping_address JSONB NOT NULL,\n    billing_address JSONB,\n    \n    -- Payment information\n    payment_status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT \'pending\',\n    payment_method_id UUID,\n    payment_method_type VARCHAR(50),\n    payment_method_name VARCHAR(100),\n    \n    -- Notes\n    customer_notes TEXT,\n    admin_notes TEXT,\n    \n    -- Timestamps\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,\n    \n    -- Metadata\n    metadata JSONB DEFAULT \'{}\'\n);\n\n-- Order items\nCREATE TABLE order_items (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    order_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    product_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES products(id),\n    quantity INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    unit_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    total_price DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    product_snapshot JSONB, -- Store product state at time of order\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Payment methods\nCREATE TABLE payment_methods (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- credit_card, bank_transfer, digital_wallet, cryptocurrency\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    provider VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    supported_currencies TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    fee_percentage DECIMAL(5,2),\n    fee_fixed DECIMAL(15,2),\n    fee_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT \'USD\',\n    min_limit DECIMAL(15,2),\n    max_limit DECIMAL(15,2),\n    limit_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT \'USD\',\n    processing_time VARCHAR(50),\n    availability TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    features TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    icon VARCHAR(10),\n    color VARCHAR(20),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Transactions\nCREATE TABLE transactions (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    reference VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    type transaction_type NOT NULL,\n    status payment_status NOT NULL,\n    amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    currency VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,\n    usd_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL, -- Always store USD equivalent\n    \n    -- Payment method\n    payment_method_id UUID REFERENCES payment_methods(id),\n    payment_method_type VARCHAR(50),\n    payment_method_name VARCHAR(100),\n    payment_method_last4 VARCHAR(4),\n    \n    -- Associated records\n    order_id UUID REFERENCES orders(id),\n    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),\n    \n    -- Fees\n    processing_fee DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    platform_fee DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    total_fee DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    net_amount DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    \n    -- Description\n    description TEXT,\n    metadata JSONB DEFAULT \'{}\',\n    \n    -- Gateway information\n    gateway_provider VARCHAR(100),\n    gateway_transaction_id VARCHAR(255),\n    gateway_authorization_code VARCHAR(100),\n    \n    -- Risk assessment\n    risk_score INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    risk_level VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT \'low\',\n    risk_flags TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    \n    -- Refund information\n    refund_amount DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    refund_reason VARCHAR(255),\n    refund_status VARCHAR(50),\n    \n    -- Timestamps\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE\n);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- SHIPPING AND DELIVERY TABLES\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Carriers\nCREATE TABLE carriers (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- express, standard, economy, freight\n    services TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    coverage TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    rating DECIMAL(3,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    reviews_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    contact_phone VARCHAR(50),\n    contact_email VARCHAR(255),\n    website VARCHAR(500),\n    \n    -- Pricing\n    base_rate DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    per_kg_rate DECIMAL(10,4),\n    per_km_rate DECIMAL(10,4),\n    fuel_surcharge DECIMAL(5,2),\n    \n    -- Features and availability\n    features TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    is_available BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    \n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Shipments\nCREATE TABLE shipments (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    tracking_number VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    order_id UUID REFERENCES orders(id),\n    shipment_reference VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    \n    -- Status\n    status shipment_status NOT NULL,\n    \n    -- Carrier information\n    carrier_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES carriers(id),\n    carrier_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    carrier_type VARCHAR(50),\n    \n    -- Route information\n    origin_address JSONB NOT NULL,\n    origin_city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    origin_country VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    origin_postal_code VARCHAR(20),\n    origin_latitude DECIMAL(10, 8),\n    origin_longitude DECIMAL(11, 8),\n    \n    destination_address JSONB NOT NULL,\n    destination_city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    destination_country VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    destination_postal_code VARCHAR(20),\n    destination_latitude DECIMAL(10, 8),\n    destination_longitude DECIMAL(11, 8),\n    \n    -- Recipient information\n    recipient_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    recipient_phone VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,\n    recipient_email VARCHAR(255),\n    \n    -- Package information\n    package_weight DECIMAL(10,3) NOT NULL,\n    package_length DECIMAL(10,2),\n    package_width DECIMAL(10,2),\n    package_height DECIMAL(10,2),\n    package_description TEXT,\n    package_value DECIMAL(15,2),\n    package_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT \'USD\',\n    insurance BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    \n    -- Shipping details\n    shipping_method VARCHAR(100),\n    shipping_cost DECIMAL(15,2),\n    estimated_delivery DATE,\n    actual_delivery DATE,\n    service_type VARCHAR(50),\n    \n    -- Current tracking\n    current_location VARCHAR(255),\n    delay_reason TEXT,\n    \n    -- Costs\n    shipping_cost_actual DECIMAL(15,2),\n    insurance_cost DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    customs_cost DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    tax_cost DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    fuel_cost DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    handling_cost DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0.00,\n    total_cost DECIMAL(15,2) NOT NULL,\n    cost_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT \'USD\',\n    \n    -- Documents\n    invoice_url VARCHAR(500),\n    customs_form_url VARCHAR(500),\n    packing_list_url VARCHAR(500),\n    certificate_url VARCHAR(500),\n    \n    -- Notes\n    notes TEXT,\n    \n    -- Timestamps\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Tracking events\nCREATE TABLE tracking_events (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    shipment_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES shipments(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,\n    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,\n    location VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    latitude DECIMAL(10, 8),\n    longitude DECIMAL(11, 8),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- REWARDS AND ACHIEVEMENTS TABLES\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Reward rules\nCREATE TABLE reward_rules (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- purchase, referral, review, social, login, milestone, custom\n    points INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    multiplier DECIMAL(3,2),\n    \n    -- Conditions\n    min_amount DECIMAL(15,2),\n    category VARCHAR(100),\n    max_per_day INTEGER,\n    max_per_month INTEGER,\n    verification_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    \n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    expiry_date DATE,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Reward activities\nCREATE TABLE reward_activities (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    rule_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES reward_rules(id),\n    rule_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    points INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT \'pending\',\n    metadata JSONB DEFAULT \'{}\',\n    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Achievements\nCREATE TABLE achievements (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    icon VARCHAR(10),\n    points INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    rarity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT \'common\',\n    target_value INTEGER,\n    rule_type VARCHAR(50),\n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- User achievements\nCREATE TABLE user_achievements (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    achievement_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES achievements(id),\n    progress_current INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    unlocked_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    UNIQUE(user_id, achievement_id)\n);\n\n-- Reward redemptions\nCREATE TABLE reward_redemptions (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT,\n    points_cost INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- discount, voucher, product, service, experience\n    category VARCHAR(50),\n    image_url VARCHAR(500),\n    value DECIMAL(15,2),\n =================================================================\n-- NEWS AND CONTENT TABLES\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- News sources\nCREATE TABLE news_sources (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    url VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,\n    country VARCHAR(100),\n    category VARCHAR(50),\n    reliability INTEGER CHECK (reliability >= 1 AND reliability <= 10),\n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- News articles\nCREATE TABLE news_articles (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,\n    summary TEXT,\n    content TEXT,\n    url VARCHAR(1000) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    \n    -- Source information\n    source_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES news_sources(id),\n    source_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    source_logo VARCHAR(500),\n    source_country VARCHAR(100),\n    \n    -- Author and publication\n    author VARCHAR(255),\n    published_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,\n    \n    -- Categories and tags\n    category VARCHAR(100),\n    tags TEXT[] DEFAULT ARRAY[],\n    \n    -- Engagement metrics\n    views INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    shares INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    comments INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    likes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,\n    \n    -- Sentiment analysis\n    sentiment VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT \'neutral\',\n    importance INTEGER CHECK (importance >= 1 AND importance <= 10) DEFAULT 5,\n    \n    -- Media\n    image_url VARCHAR(1000),\n    \n    -- User interactions\n    is_bookmarked BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    is_read BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    \n    -- Timestamps\n    scraped_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- PROXY AND NETWORK TABLES\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Proxy nodes\nCREATE TABLE proxy_nodes (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    ip_address INET NOT NULL,\n    port INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    country VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    city VARCHAR(100),\n    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- tor, vpn, socks5, http, https\n    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT \'offline\',\n    latency INTEGER DEFAULT 0, -- milliseconds\n    bandwidth DECIMAL(10,2), -- MB/s\n    uptime DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0.00, -- percentage\n    last_checked TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    anonymity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT \'medium\',\n    encryption BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    logs_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    traffic_used BIGINT DEFAULT 0,\n    traffic_limit BIGINT DEFAULT 0,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- SYSTEM CONFIGURATION TABLES\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Currencies\nCREATE TABLE currencies (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    code VARCHAR(3) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    symbol VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,\n    rate DECIMAL(20,8) NOT NULL, -- Rate to USD\n    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,\n    is_default BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    decimal_places INTEGER DEFAULT 2,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- System settings\nCREATE TABLE system_settings (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    key VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n    value TEXT,\n    description TEXT,\n    is_public BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Audit logs\nCREATE TABLE audit_logs (\n    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),\n    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),\n    action VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,\n    table_name VARCHAR(100),\n    record_id UUID,\n    old_values JSONB,\n    new_values JSONB,\n    ip_address INET,\n    user_agent TEXT,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- INDEXES FOR PERFORMANCE\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Users indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_status ON users(status);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_country ON users(country);\nCREATE INDEX idx_users_city ON users(city);\n\n-- Products indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_supplier_id ON products(supplier_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_category_id ON products(category_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_is_active ON products(is_active);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_price ON products(price);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_rating ON products(rating);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_created_at ON products(created_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_products_tags ON products USING GIN(tags);\n\n-- Orders indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_orders_user_id ON orders(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_orders_status ON orders(status);\nCREATE INDEX idx_orders_created_at ON orders(created_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_orders_total_amount ON orders(total_amount);\n\n-- Transactions indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_user_id ON transactions(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_order_id ON transactions(order_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_status ON transactions(status);\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_type ON transactions(type);\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_created_at ON transactions(created_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_transactions_amount ON transactions(amount);\n\n-- Shipments indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_shipments_order_id ON shipments(order_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_shipments_carrier_id ON shipments(carrier_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_shipments_status ON shipments(status);\nCREATE INDEX idx_shipments_tracking_number ON shipments(tracking_number);\nCREATE INDEX idx_shipments_created_at ON shipments(created_at);\n\n-- Tracking events indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_tracking_events_shipment_id ON tracking_events(shipment_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_tracking_events_timestamp ON tracking_events(timestamp);\n\n-- News articles indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_news_articles_source_id ON news_articles(source_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_news_articles_published_at ON news_articles(published_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_news_articles_category ON news_articles(category);\nCREATE INDEX idx_news_articles_sentiment ON news_articles(sentiment);\nCREATE INDEX idx_news_articles_tags ON news_articles USING GIN(tags);\n\n-- Reward activities indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_reward_activities_user_id ON reward_activities(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_reward_activities_created_at ON reward_activities(created_at);\n\n-- User rewards indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_user_rewards_user_id ON user_rewards(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_user_rewards_current_tier ON user_rewards(current_tier);\n\n-- Audit logs indexes\nCREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_user_id ON audit_logs(user_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_action ON audit_logs(action);\nCREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_created_at ON audit_logs(created_at);\nCREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_table_name ON audit_logs(table_name);\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- TRIGGERS AND FUNCTIONS\n-- =================================================================\n\n-- Function to update updated_at timestamp\nCREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()\nRETURNS TRIGGER AS $$\nBEGIN\n    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;\n    RETURN NEW;\nEND;\n$$ language \'plpgsql\';\n\n-- Create triggers for updated_at\nCREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON users\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\nCREATE TRIGGER update_products_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON products\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\nCREATE TRIGGER update_orders_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON orders\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\nCREATE TRIGGER update_transactions_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON transactions\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\nCREATE TRIGGER update_shipments_updated_at BEFORE UPDATE ON shipments\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();\n\n-- Function to update user statistics\nCREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_user_statistics()\nRETURNS TRIGGER AS $$\nBEGIN\n    IF TG_OP = \'INSERT\' THEN\n        INSERT INTO user_statistics (user_id) VALUES (NEW.user_id)\n        ON CONFLICT (user_id) DO NOTHING;\n        RETURN NEW;\n    END IF;\n    \n    IF TG_OP = \'UPDATE\' THEN\n        -- Update order statistics when order is completed\n        IF OLD.status != \'completed\' AND NEW.status = \'completed\' THEN\n            UPDATE user_statistics SET\n                total_orders = total_orders + 1,\n                total_spent = total_spent + NEW.total_amount,\n                updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n            WHERE user_id = NEW.user_id;\n        END IF;\n        RETURN NEW;\n    END IF;\n    \n    RETURN NULL;\nEND;\n$$ language \'plpgsql\';\n\n-- Create trigger for user statistics\nCREATE TRIGGER update_user_stats_trigger\n    AFTER INSERT OR UPDATE ON orders\n    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_user_statistics();\n\n-- =================================================================\n-- INITIAL DATA INSERTION\n-- =================================================================\n\n--
